[stdout]   # Agents and Subagents
[stdout]   An agent defines the AI's behavior, including system prompts, available tools, and subagents. You can use built-in agents or create custom agents.
[stdout]   ## Built-in agents
[stdout]   Kimi Code CLI provides two built-in agents. You can select one at startup with the `--agent` flag:
[stdout]   ```sh
[stdout]   kimi --agent okabe
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   ### `default`
[stdout]   The default agent, suitable for general use. Enabled tools:
[stdout]   `Agent`, `AskUserQuestion`, `SetTodoList`, `Shell`, `ReadFile`, `ReadMediaFile`, `Glob`, `Grep`, `WriteFile`, `StrReplaceFile`, `SearchWeb`, `FetchURL`, `EnterPlanMode`, `ExitPlanMode`, `TaskList`, `TaskOutput`, `TaskStop`
[stdout]   ### `okabe`
[stdout]   An experimental agent for testing new prompts and tools. Adds `SendDMail` on top of `default`.
[stdout]   ## Custom agent files
[stdout]   Agents are defined in YAML format. Load a custom agent with the `--agent-file` flag:
[stdout]   ```sh
[stdout]   kimi --agent-file /path/to/my-agent.yaml
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   **Basic structure**
[stdout]   ```yaml
[stdout]   version: 1
[stdout]   agent:
[stdout]     name: my-agent
[stdout]     system_prompt_path: ./system.md
[stdout]     tools:
[stdout]       - "kimi_cli.tools.shell:Shell"
[stdout]       - "kimi_cli.tools.file:ReadFile"
[stdout]       - "kimi_cli.tools.file:WriteFile"
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   **Inheritance and overrides**
[stdout]   Use `extend` to inherit another agent's configuration and only override what you need to change:
[stdout]   ```yaml
[stdout]   version: 1
[stdout]   agent:
[stdout]     extend: default  # Inherit from default agent
[stdout]     system_prompt_path: ./my-prompt.md  # Override system prompt
[stdout]     exclude_tools:  # Exclude certain tools
[stdout]       - "kimi_cli.tools.web:SearchWeb"
[stdout]       - "kimi_cli.tools.web:FetchURL"
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   `extend: default` inherits from the built-in default agent. You can also specify a relative path to inherit from another agent file.
[stdout]   **Configuration fields**
[stdout]   | Field | Description | Required |
[stdout]   |-------|-------------|----------|
[stdout]   | `extend` | Agent to inherit from, can be `default` or a relative path | No |
[stdout]   | `name` | Agent name | Yes (optional when inheriting) |
[stdout]   | `system_prompt_path` | System prompt file path, relative to agent file | Yes (optional when inheriting) |
[stdout]   | `system_prompt_args` | Custom arguments passed to system prompt, merged when inheriting | No |
[stdout]   | `tools` | Tool list, format is `module:ClassName` | Yes (optional when inheriting) |
[stdout]   | `exclude_tools` | Tools to exclude | No |
[stdout]   | `subagents` | Subagent definitions | No |
[stdout]   ## System prompt built-in parameters
[stdout]   The system prompt file is a Markdown template that can use `${VAR}` syntax to reference variables and supports the Jinja2 `{% include %}` directive to include other files. Built-in variables include:
[stdout]   | Variable | Description |
[stdout]   |----------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `${KIMI_NOW}` | Current time (ISO format) |
[stdout]   | `${KIMI_WORK_DIR}` | Working directory path |
[stdout]   | `${KIMI_WORK_DIR_LS}` | Working directory file list |
[stdout]   | `${KIMI_AGENTS_MD}` | Merged `AGENTS.md` content from project root to working directory (including `.kimi/AGENTS.md`) |
[stdout]   | `${KIMI_SKILLS}` | Loaded skills list |
[stdout]   | `${KIMI_ADDITIONAL_DIRS_INFO}` | Information about additional directories added via `--add-dir` or `/add-dir` |
[stdout]   You can also define custom parameters via `system_prompt_args`:
[stdout]   ```yaml
[stdout]   agent:
[stdout]     system_prompt_args:
[stdout]       MY_VAR: "custom value"
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   Then use `${MY_VAR}` in the prompt.
[stdout]   **System prompt example**
[stdout]   ```markdown
[stdout]   # My Agent
[stdout]   You are a helpful assistant. Current time: ${KIMI_NOW}.
[stdout]   Working directory: ${KIMI_WORK_DIR}
[stdout]   ${MY_VAR}
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   ## Defining subagents in agent files
[stdout]   Subagents can handle specific types of tasks. After defining subagents in an agent file, the main agent can launch them via the `Agent` tool:
[stdout]   ```yaml
[stdout]   version: 1
[stdout]   agent:
[stdout]     extend: default
[stdout]     subagents:
[stdout]       coder:
[stdout]         path: ./coder.yaml
[stdout]         description: "Handle coding tasks"
[stdout]       reviewer:
[stdout]         path: ./reviewer.yaml
[stdout]         description: "Code review expert"
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   Subagent files are also standard agent format, typically inheriting from the main agent:
[stdout]   ```yaml
[stdout]   # coder.yaml
[stdout]   version: 1
[stdout]   agent:
[stdout]     extend: ./agent.yaml  # Inherit from main agent
[stdout]     system_prompt_args:
[stdout]       ROLE_ADDITIONAL: |
[stdout]         You are now running as a subagent...
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   ## Built-in subagent types
[stdout]   The default agent configuration includes three built-in subagent types, each with different tool policies and use cases:
[stdout]   | Type | Purpose | Available tools |
[stdout]   |------|---------|----------------|
[stdout]   | `coder` | General software engineering: read/write files, run commands, search code | `Shell`, `ReadFile`, `Glob`, `Grep`, `WriteFile`, `StrReplaceFile`, `SearchWeb`, `FetchURL` |
[stdout]   | `explore` | Fast read-only codebase exploration: search, read, summarize | `Shell`, `ReadFile`, `Glob`, `Grep`, `SearchWeb`, `FetchURL` (no write tools) |
[stdout]   | `plan` | Implementation planning and architecture design: analyze files, create plans | `ReadFile`, `Glob`, `Grep`, `SearchWeb`, `FetchURL` (no Shell, no write tools) |
[stdout]   All subagent types are prohibited from nesting the `Agent` tool (subagents cannot create their own subagents). The `Agent` tool is only available to the root agent.
[stdout]   ## How subagents run
[stdout]   Subagents launched via the `Agent` tool run in an isolated context and return results to the main agent when complete. Each subagent instance maintains its own context history and metadata under `subagents/<agent_id>/` in the session directory, and can be resumed across multiple invocations. Advantages of this approach:
[stdout]   * Isolated context, avoiding pollution of main agent's conversation history
[stdout]   * Multiple independent tasks can be processed in parallel
[stdout]   * Subagents can have targeted system prompts
[stdout]   * Persistent instances preserve context across multiple calls
[stdout]   ## Built-in tools list
[stdout]   The following are all built-in tools in Kimi Code CLI.
[stdout]   ### `Agent`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.agent:Agent`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Start or resume a subagent instance for a focused task. Three built-in subagent types are available: `coder` (general software engineering), `explore` (fast read-only codebase exploration), and `plan` (implementation planning and architecture design). Each instance maintains its own context history and supports foreground or background execution.
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `description` | string | Short task description (3-5 words) |
[stdout]   | `prompt` | string | Detailed task description |
[stdout]   | `subagent_type` | string | Built-in subagent type, default `coder` |
[stdout]   | `model` | string | Optional model override |
[stdout]   | `resume` | string | Optional agent instance ID to resume an existing instance |
[stdout]   | `run_in_background` | bool | Whether to run in background, default false |
[stdout]   ### `AskUserQuestion`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.ask_user:AskUserQuestion`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Present structured questions and options to the user during execution, collecting preferences or decisions. Suitable for scenarios where the user needs to choose between approaches, resolve ambiguous instructions, or provide requirements. Should not be overused — only call when the user's choice genuinely affects subsequent actions.
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `questions` | array | Questions list (1–4 questions) |
[stdout]   | `questions[].question` | string | Question text, ending with `?` |
[stdout]   | `questions[].header` | string | Short label, max 12 characters (e.g., `Auth`, `Style`) |
[stdout]   | `questions[].options` | array | Available options (2–4), the system adds an "Other" option automatically |
[stdout]   | `questions[].options[].label` | string | Option label (1–5 words), append `(Recommended)` for recommended options |
[stdout]   | `questions[].options[].description` | string | Option description |
[stdout]   | `questions[].multi_select` | bool | Allow multiple selections, default false |
[stdout]   ### `SetTodoList`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.todo:SetTodoList`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Manage todo list, track task progress
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `todos` | array | Todo list items |
[stdout]   | `todos[].title` | string | Todo item title |
[stdout]   | `todos[].status` | string | Status: `pending`, `in_progress`, `done` |
[stdout]   ### `Shell`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.shell:Shell`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Execute shell commands. Requires user approval. Uses the appropriate shell for the OS (bash/zsh on Unix, PowerShell on Windows).
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `command` | string | Command to execute |
[stdout]   | `timeout` | int | Timeout in seconds, default 60, max 300 for foreground / 86400 for background |
[stdout]   | `run_in_background` | bool | Whether to run as a background task, default false |
[stdout]   | `description` | string | Short description for the background task, required when `run_in_background=true` |
[stdout]   When `run_in_background=true`, the command is launched as a background task and the tool immediately returns a task ID, allowing the AI to continue working. The system automatically sends a notification when the task completes. Ideal for long-running builds, tests, watchers, and servers.
[stdout]   ### `ReadFile`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.file:ReadFile`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Read text file content. Max 1000 lines per read, max 2000 characters per line. Files outside working directory require absolute paths. Every read returns the total number of lines in the file.
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `path` | string | File path |
[stdout]   | `line_offset` | int | Starting line number, default 1. Supports negative values to read from the end of the file (e.g. `-100` reads the last 100 lines); absolute value cannot exceed 1000 |
[stdout]   | `n_lines` | int | Number of lines to read, default/max 1000 |
[stdout]   ### `ReadMediaFile`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.file:ReadMediaFile`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Read image or video files. Max file size 100MB. Only available when the model supports image/video input. Files outside working directory require absolute paths.
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `path` | string | File path |
[stdout]   ### `Glob`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.file:Glob`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Match files and directories by pattern. Returns max 1000 matches, patterns starting with `**` not allowed. Can also search within discovered skill roots, and `~` in paths is expanded to the user's home directory.
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `pattern` | string | Glob pattern (e.g., `*.py`, `src/**/*.ts`) |
[stdout]   | `directory` | string | Search directory, defaults to working directory |
[stdout]   | `include_dirs` | bool | Include directories, default true |
[stdout]   ### `Grep`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.file:Grep`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Search file content with regular expressions, based on ripgrep
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `pattern` | string | Regular expression pattern |
[stdout]   | `path` | string | Search path, defaults to current directory |
[stdout]   | `glob` | string | File filter (e.g., `*.js`) |
[stdout]   | `type` | string | File type (e.g., `py`, `js`, `go`) |
[stdout]   | `output_mode` | string | Output mode: `files_with_matches` (default), `content`, `count_matches` |
[stdout]   | `-B` | int | Show N lines before match |
[stdout]   | `-A` | int | Show N lines after match |
[stdout]   | `-C` | int | Show N lines before and after match |
[stdout]   | `-n` | bool | Show line numbers |
[stdout]   | `-i` | bool | Case insensitive |
[stdout]   | `multiline` | bool | Enable multiline matching |
[stdout]   | `head_limit` | int | Limit output lines |
[stdout]   ### `WriteFile`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.file:WriteFile`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Write files. Requires user approval. Absolute paths are required when writing files outside the working directory.
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `path` | string | Absolute path |
[stdout]   | `content` | string | File content |
[stdout]   | `mode` | string | `overwrite` (default) or `append` |
[stdout]   ### `StrReplaceFile`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.file:StrReplaceFile`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Edit files using string replacement. Requires user approval. Absolute paths are required when editing files outside the working directory.
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `path` | string | Absolute path |
[stdout]   | `edit` | object/array | Single edit or list of edits |
[stdout]   | `edit.old` | string | Original string to replace |
[stdout]   | `edit.new` | string | Replacement string |
[stdout]   | `edit.replace_all` | bool | Replace all matches, default false |
[stdout]   ### `SearchWeb`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.web:SearchWeb`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Search the web. Requires search service configuration (auto-configured on Kimi Code platform).
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `query` | string | Search keywords |
[stdout]   | `limit` | int | Number of results, default 5, max 20 |
[stdout]   | `include_content` | bool | Include page content, default false |
[stdout]   ### `FetchURL`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.web:FetchURL`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Fetch webpage content, returns extracted main text. Uses fetch service if configured, otherwise uses local HTTP request.
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `url` | string | URL to fetch |
[stdout]   ### `Think`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.think:Think`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Let the agent record thinking process, suitable for complex reasoning scenarios
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `thought` | string | Thinking content |
[stdout]   ### `SendDMail`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.dmail:SendDMail`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Send delayed message (D-Mail), for checkpoint rollback scenarios
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `message` | string | Message to send |
[stdout]   | `checkpoint_id` | int | Checkpoint ID to send back to (>= 0) |
[stdout]   ### `EnterPlanMode`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.plan.enter:EnterPlanMode`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Request to enter plan mode. After calling, an approval request is presented to the user, who can approve or reject entering plan mode. In YOLO mode, this is only used when the user explicitly requests planning or when there is significant architectural ambiguity. See [Plan mode](../guides/interaction.md#plan-mode).
[stdout]   This tool takes no parameters.
[stdout]   ### `ExitPlanMode`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.plan:ExitPlanMode`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Submit a plan for user approval while in plan mode. Before calling, the plan must be written to the plan file. This tool reads the plan file content and presents it to the user for approval. The user can select an implementation path (exit plan mode and start execution), reject (stay in plan mode and wait for feedback), or provide revision comments. See [Plan mode](../guides/interaction.md#plan-mode).
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `options` | list | null | When the plan contains multiple alternative implementation paths, list 2–3 options for the user to choose from. Each option has a `label` (1–8 word short name, may append "(Recommended)") and an optional `description` (brief summary). The labels "Approve", "Reject", and "Revise" are reserved and cannot be used. |
[stdout]   ### `TaskList`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.background:TaskList`
[stdout]   * **Description**: List background tasks in the current session. Useful for re-enumerating task IDs after context compaction or checking which tasks are still running.
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `active_only` | bool | List only active tasks, default true |
[stdout]   | `limit` | int | Maximum number of tasks to return (1–100), default 20 |
[stdout]   ### `TaskOutput`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.background:TaskOutput`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Retrieve output and status of a background task. Returns a non-blocking status/output snapshot by default; use `ReadFile` with the returned `output_path` to read the full log if output is truncated.
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `task_id` | string | Task ID to query |
[stdout]   | `block` | bool | Whether to wait for task completion, default false |
[stdout]   | `timeout` | int | Maximum wait time in seconds when `block=true` (0–3600), default 30 |
[stdout]   ### `TaskStop`
[stdout]   * **Path**: `kimi_cli.tools.background:TaskStop`
[stdout]   * **Description**: Stop a running background task. Requires user approval. Use only when a task must be cancelled; for normal completion, wait for the automatic notification. Not available in plan mode.
[stdout]   | Parameter | Type | Description |
[stdout]   |-----------|------|-------------|
[stdout]   | `task_id` | string | Task ID to stop |
[stdout]   | `reason` | string | Reason for stopping (optional), default "Stopped by TaskStop" |
[stdout]   ## Tool security boundaries
[stdout]   **Workspace scope**
[stdout]   * File reading and writing are typically done within the working directory (and additional directories added via `--add-dir` or `/add-dir`)
[stdout]   * Absolute paths are required when reading files outside the workspace
[stdout]   * Write and edit operations require user approval; absolute paths are required when operating on files outside the workspace
[stdout]   **Approval mechanism**
[stdout]   The following operations require user approval:
[stdout]   | Operation | Approval required |
[stdout]   |-----------|-------------------|
[stdout]   | Shell command execution | Each execution |
[stdout]   | File write/edit | Each operation |
[stdout]   | MCP tool calls | Each call |
[stdout]   | Stop background task | Each stop |

[stdout]   # Config Files
[stdout]   Kimi Code CLI uses configuration files to manage API providers, models, services, and runtime parameters, supporting both TOML and JSON formats.
[stdout]   ## Config file location
[stdout]   The default configuration file is located at `~/.kimi/config.toml`. On first run, if the configuration file doesn't exist, Kimi Code CLI will automatically create a default configuration file.
[stdout]   You can specify a different configuration file (TOML or JSON format) with the `--config-file` flag:
[stdout]   ```sh
[stdout]   kimi --config-file /path/to/config.toml
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   When calling Kimi Code CLI programmatically, you can also pass the complete configuration content directly via the `--config` flag:
[stdout]   ```sh
[stdout]   kimi --config '{"default_model": "kimi-for-coding", "providers": {...}, "models": {...}}'
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   ## Config items
[stdout]   The configuration file contains the following top-level configuration items:
[stdout]   | Item | Type | Description |
[stdout]   | --- | --- | --- |
[stdout]   | `default_model` | `string` | Default model name, must be a model defined in `models` |
[stdout]   | `default_thinking` | `boolean` | Whether to enable thinking mode by default (defaults to `false`) |
[stdout]   | `default_yolo` | `boolean` | Whether to enable YOLO (auto-approve) mode by default (defaults to `false`) |
[stdout]   | `default_plan_mode` | `boolean` | Whether to start new sessions in plan mode by default (defaults to `false`); resumed sessions preserve their existing state |
[stdout]   | `default_editor` | `string` | Default external editor command (e.g. `"vim"`, `"code --wait"`), auto-detects when empty |
[stdout]   | `theme` | `string` | Terminal color theme, either `"dark"` or `"light"` (defaults to `"dark"`) |
[stdout]   | `merge_all_available_skills` | `boolean` | Whether to merge skills from all brand directories (defaults to `false`); see [Skills configuration](../customization/skills.md) |
[stdout]   | `providers` | `table` | API provider configuration |
[stdout]   | `models` | `table` | Model configuration |
[stdout]   | `loop_control` | `table` | Agent loop control parameters |
[stdout]   | `background` | `table` | Background task runtime parameters |
[stdout]   | `services` | `table` | External service configuration (search, fetch) |
[stdout]   | `mcp` | `table` | MCP client configuration |
[stdout]   ### Complete configuration example
[stdout]   ```toml
[stdout]   default_model = "kimi-for-coding"
[stdout]   default_thinking = false
[stdout]   default_yolo = false
[stdout]   default_plan_mode = false
[stdout]   default_editor = ""
[stdout]   theme = "dark"
[stdout]   merge_all_available_skills = false
[stdout]   [providers.kimi-for-coding]
[stdout]   type = "kimi"
[stdout]   base_url = "https://api.kimi.com/coding/v1"
[stdout]   api_key = "sk-xxx"
[stdout]   [models.kimi-for-coding]
[stdout]   provider = "kimi-for-coding"
[stdout]   model = "kimi-for-coding"
[stdout]   max_context_size = 262144
[stdout]   [loop_control]
[stdout]   max_steps_per_turn = 100
[stdout]   max_retries_per_step = 3
[stdout]   max_ralph_iterations = 0
[stdout]   reserved_context_size = 50000
[stdout]   compaction_trigger_ratio = 0.85
[stdout]   [background]
[stdout]   max_running_tasks = 4
[stdout]   keep_alive_on_exit = false
[stdout]   agent_task_timeout_s = 900
[stdout]   [services.moonshot_search]
[stdout]   base_url = "https://api.kimi.com/coding/v1/search"
[stdout]   api_key = "sk-xxx"
[stdout]   [services.moonshot_fetch]
[stdout]   base_url = "https://api.kimi.com/coding/v1/fetch"
[stdout]   api_key = "sk-xxx"
[stdout]   [mcp.client]
[stdout]   tool_call_timeout_ms = 60000
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   ### `providers`
[stdout]   `providers` defines API provider connection information. Each provider uses a unique name as key.
[stdout]   | Field | Type | Required | Description |
[stdout]   | --- | --- | --- | --- |
[stdout]   | `type` | `string` | Yes | Provider type, see [Providers](./providers.md) for details |
[stdout]   | `base_url` | `string` | Yes | API base URL |
[stdout]   | `api_key` | `string` | Yes | API key |
[stdout]   | `env` | `table` | No | Environment variables to set before creating provider instance |
[stdout]   | `custom_headers` | `table` | No | Custom HTTP headers to attach to requests |
[stdout]   Example:
[stdout]   ```toml
[stdout]   [providers.moonshot-cn]
[stdout]   type = "kimi"
[stdout]   base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1"
[stdout]   api_key = "sk-xxx"
[stdout]   custom_headers = { "X-Custom-Header" = "value" }
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   ### `models`
[stdout]   `models` defines available models. Each model uses a unique name as key.
[stdout]   | Field | Type | Required | Description |
[stdout]   | --- | --- | --- | --- |
[stdout]   | `provider` | `string` | Yes | Provider name to use, must be defined in `providers` |
[stdout]   | `model` | `string` | Yes | Model identifier (model name used in API) |
[stdout]   | `max_context_size` | `integer` | Yes | Maximum context length (in tokens) |
[stdout]   | `capabilities` | `array` | No | Model capability list, see [Providers](./providers.md#model-capabilities) for details |
[stdout]   Example:
[stdout]   ```toml
[stdout]   [models.kimi-k2-thinking-turbo]
[stdout]   provider = "moonshot-cn"
[stdout]   model = "kimi-k2-thinking-turbo"
[stdout]   max_context_size = 262144
[stdout]   capabilities = ["thinking", "image_in"]
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   ### `loop_control`
[stdout]   `loop_control` controls agent execution loop behavior.
[stdout]   | Field | Type | Default | Description |
[stdout]   | --- | --- | --- | --- |
[stdout]   | `max_steps_per_turn` | `integer` | `100` | Maximum steps per turn (alias: `max_steps_per_run`) |
[stdout]   | `max_retries_per_step` | `integer` | `3` | Maximum retries per step |
[stdout]   | `max_ralph_iterations` | `integer` | `0` | Extra iterations after each user message; `0` disables; `-1` is unlimited |
[stdout]   | `reserved_context_size` | `integer` | `50000` | Reserved token count for LLM response generation; auto-compaction triggers when `context_tokens + reserved_context_size >= max_context_size` |
[stdout]   | `compaction_trigger_ratio` | `float` | `0.85` | Context usage ratio threshold for auto-compaction (0.5–0.99); auto-compaction triggers when `context_tokens >= max_context_size * compaction_trigger_ratio`, whichever condition is met first with `reserved_context_size` |
[stdout]   ### `background`
[stdout]   `background` controls background task runtime behavior. Background tasks are launched via the `Shell` tool or the `Agent` tool with `run_in_background=true`.
[stdout]   | Field | Type | Default | Description |
[stdout]   | --- | --- | --- | --- |
[stdout]   | `max_running_tasks` | `integer` | `4` | Maximum number of concurrent background tasks |
[stdout]   | `keep_alive_on_exit` | `boolean` | `false` | Whether to keep background tasks running when CLI exits; default is to terminate all background tasks on exit |
[stdout]   | `agent_task_timeout_s` | `integer` | `900` | Maximum runtime in seconds for a background agent task; timed-out tasks are marked as failed and the main agent is notified |
[stdout]   ### `services`
[stdout]   `services` configures external services used by Kimi Code CLI.
[stdout]   #### `moonshot_search`
[stdout]   Configures web search service. When enabled, the `SearchWeb` tool becomes available.
[stdout]   | Field | Type | Required | Description |
[stdout]   | --- | --- | --- | --- |
[stdout]   | `base_url` | `string` | Yes | Search service API URL |
[stdout]   | `api_key` | `string` | Yes | API key |
[stdout]   | `custom_headers` | `table` | No | Custom HTTP headers to attach to requests |
[stdout]   #### `moonshot_fetch`
[stdout]   Configures web fetch service. When enabled, the `FetchURL` tool prioritizes using this service to fetch webpage content.
[stdout]   | Field | Type | Required | Description |
[stdout]   | --- | --- | --- | --- |
[stdout]   | `base_url` | `string` | Yes | Fetch service API URL |
[stdout]   | `api_key` | `string` | Yes | API key |
[stdout]   | `custom_headers` | `table` | No | Custom HTTP headers to attach to requests |
[stdout]   ::: tip
[stdout]   When configuring the Kimi Code platform using the `/login` command, search and fetch services are automatically configured.
[stdout]   :::
[stdout]   ### `mcp`
[stdout]   `mcp` configures MCP client behavior.
[stdout]   | Field | Type | Default | Description |
[stdout]   | --- | --- | --- | --- |
[stdout]   | `client.tool_call_timeout_ms` | `integer` | `60000` | MCP tool call timeout (milliseconds) |
[stdout]   ### `hooks`
[stdout]   `hooks` configures lifecycle hooks (Beta feature). See [Hooks](../customization/hooks.md) for details.
[stdout]   Use the `[[hooks]]` array syntax to define multiple hooks:
[stdout]   ```toml
[stdout]   [[hooks]]
[stdout]   event = "PreToolUse"
[stdout]   matcher = "Shell"
[stdout]   command = ".kimi/hooks/safety-check.sh"
[stdout]   timeout = 10
[stdout]   [[hooks]]
[stdout]   event = "PostToolUse"
[stdout]   matcher = "WriteFile"
[stdout]   command = "prettier --write"
[stdout]   ```
[stdout]   | Field | Type | Required | Description |
[stdout]   | --- | --- | --- | --- |
[stdout]   | `event` | `string` | Yes | Event type, e.g., `PreToolUse`, `Stop`, etc. |
[stdout]   | `command` | `string` | Yes | Shell command to execute |
[stdout]   | `matcher` | `string` | No | Regex filter condition |
[stdout]   | `timeout` | `integer` | No | Timeout in seconds, default 30 |
[stdout]   ## JSON configuration migration
[stdout]   If `~/.kimi/config.toml` doesn't exist but `~/.kimi/config.json` exists, Kimi Code CLI will automatically migrate the JSON configuration to TOML format and backup the original file as `config.json.bak`.
[stdout]   `--config-file` specified configuration files are parsed based on file extension. `--config` passed configuration content is first attempted as JSON, then falls back to TOML if that fails.
